##Ludwig the German and his sons
#Ludwig the German
90107 = {
	name = "Ludwig"
	dna = 90107_ludwig_the_german
	# AKA: Ludwig 'der Deutsche'
	dynasty = 25061
	martial = 6
	diplomacy = 5
	intrigue = 7
	stewardship = 5
	religion = "catholic"
	culture = franconian
	trait = education_martial_1
	trait = ambitious
	trait = stubborn
	trait = trusting
	sexuality = heterosexual					 
	father = 90095
	mother = 91002
	806.1.1 = {
		birth = yes
		effect = {
			add_character_flag = has_scripted_appearance
		}
	}
	826.1.1 = {
		set_primary_title_to = title:k_east_francia
	}
	827.1.1 = {
		add_spouse = 7987 #Hemma
		give_nickname = nick_the_pious #'the German' is an 18th century nickname. His contemporaries gave him the epithet pious
	}
	867.1.1 = {
		remove_claim = title:e_hre
		effect = { set_designated_heir = character:42019 }											
	}
	876.1.29 = {
		death = yes
	}
}

#Karlmann of Bavaria
42018 = {
	name = "Karlmann"
	dynasty = 25061
	martial = 8
	diplomacy = 5
	intrigue = 3
	stewardship = 5
	learning = 8
	religion = "catholic"
	culture = franconian
	trait = education_martial_4
	trait = greedy
	trait = zealous
	trait = humble
	trait = ill
	sexuality = heterosexual					 
	father = 90107 #(Ludwig the German)
	mother = 7987
	830.1.14 = {
		birth = yes
	}
	846.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			set_relation_friend = { reason = friend_generic_history target = character:7987 } #His mother Hemma, he was her favorite
		}
	}
	850.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			set_relation_lover = { reason = lover_history target = character:167813 } # Liutswind
			set_relation_rival = { reason = rival_historical target = character:167812 } # Liutswind's brother, Ernst
		}
	}
	860.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			set_relation_rival = { reason = rival_historical target = character:90107 }
			add_opinion = {
				target = character:90107 #Karlmann had a "conflictual" relationship with his father
				modifier = hate_opinion
				opinion = -200
			}
		}
	}
	866.1.1 = {
		add_spouse = 167813# Liutswind
	}
	867.1.1 = {
        contract_disease_effect = { DISEASE = ill TREATMENT_EVENT = yes }
	}
	880.9.29 = {
		death = yes
	}
}
